< Text>
Who would have thought that among Temecula, Menifee and Hemet, Hemet would beat hands down the best bakery challenge? Tried them all, at least once, and yesterday after reading somewhere of the Harvard St Bakery and Cafe, I decided to go out of my comfort zone to Hemet to try the place. Yes, it took about 17 minutes each way, but the end results was well worth it.
In what appeared a downtown area resides this bakery. Grace took my order, and later Rose?, the owner, and apparently the one with the magic touch, appeared as well. Both extremely pleasant ladies, making the first time shopping experience a very nice one.
Bought a couple of breads, since at 2 in the afternoon on a Saturday, were the last to be found, no baguettes to be had. Also purchased several pastries, including a very delicious Banana Bread Pudding, with probably the best icing to put on top, given on the side. Very creamy, not too sweet, which kind of told the story of this place. If the icing is made with so much pride, then definitely this bakery, like good cream, rises to the top. The owner said that she could, and would prepare, most special requests, as I mentioned Dulce de Leche creations. I am also thinking about a German Apple Strudel with thin crust, and fresh apples.
One would think that I was a spring chicken, with unlimited capacity for good sweets, but that certainly is not the case, for we all, as a family do crave superior baked items, and when we are lucky to find a decent bakery we love it! Hard to find good quality, and we really enjoyed most of the selected pastries. Better than a Donut Shop, that‚Äôs for sure, since the products are not saturated with sugars to the point of no return. 4.5 Stars.</Text>

< review>
In short, the food is great if you like Filipino food with a twist. I recommend getting the fusion dishes and not the typical Filipino food. The service is very positive (it's a family business).
I went with my parents (both Filipino) for the first time. I ordered the adobo fries, my mom got the adobo bowl, and my dad got the MK combo. The putoflan was very good, the ube cupcake was good, and the fruit pizza (with a cookie base) was very sweet (I liked it).<//review>

We love Eurekas food and will definitely be dining with them again.  A BIG SHOUT OUT TO SID FOR GREAT CUSTOMER SERVICE!<//text>

The beat burgers are amazing. Unfortunately, the buns are not vegan (come on Eureka!) so vegans will need to replace the bun with an arugula salad (it's pretty good, but sometimes you just want a real burger). The protein salad is delicious and cheap. The happy hour is every day before 6pm and after 9pm. They sometimes have Brussels sprouts with a balasic glaze which are amazing. The staff is generally very friendly but it seems like there is a lot of turn over in the staff. Anyway, if you're a cool person, go here. Great beer, good prices, great location.</Text>< userid>
